# Modular arithmetic

## The congruence class of a natural number modulo a successor

<pre class="Agda"><a id="mod-succ-ℕ"></a><a id="2844" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="2855" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2857" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2858" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2858" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="2860" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2862" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="2863" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2865" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2867" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="2869" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2871" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="2875" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2876" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="2883" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2858" class="Bound">k</a><a id="2884" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="2886" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="2897" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2897" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="2899" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1479" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕ</a> <a id="2906" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2908" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7083" class="Function">zero-Fin</a>
<a id="2917" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="2928" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2928" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="2930" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2931" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="2938" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2938" class="Bound">n</a><a id="2939" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2941" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2943" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7668" class="Function">succ-Fin</a> <a id="2952" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2953" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="2964" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2928" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="2966" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2938" class="Bound">n</a><a id="2967" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="mod-two-ℕ"></a><a id="2970" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2970" class="Function">mod-two-ℕ</a> <a id="2980" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2982" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="2984" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2986" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="2990" class="Number">2</a>
<a id="2992" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2970" class="Function">mod-two-ℕ</a> <a id="3002" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3004" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="3015" class="Number">1</a>

<a id="mod-three-ℕ"></a><a id="3018" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3018" class="Function">mod-three-ℕ</a> <a id="3030" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3032" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3034" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3036" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="3040" class="Number">3</a>
<a id="3042" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3018" class="Function">mod-three-ℕ</a> <a id="3054" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3056" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="3067" class="Number">2</a>
</pre>

  <a id="3220" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#2763" class="Function">cong-identification-ℕ</a>
    <a id="3246" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="3248" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="3255" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3205" class="Bound">k</a><a id="3256" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="3410" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="3412" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="3419" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3366" class="Bound">k</a><a id="3420" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="3426" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="3428" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="3436" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3437" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="3444" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3366" class="Bound">k</a><a id="3445" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3447" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7083" class="Function">zero-Fin</a><a id="3455" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="3461" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="3463" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1479" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕ</a><a id="3469" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="3475" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="3477" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="3484" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3366" class="Bound">k</a><a id="3485" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="3491" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="3493" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7884" class="Function">is-zero-nat-zero-Fin</a> <a id="3514" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3515" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3366" class="Bound">k</a><a id="3516" class="Symbol">})</a>
    <a id="3523" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="3525" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#3044" class="Function">cong-zero-ℕ&#39;</a> <a id="3538" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3539" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="3546" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3366" class="Bound">k</a><a id="3547" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="cong-nat-mod-succ-ℕ"></a><a id="3551" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3551" class="Function">cong-nat-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="3571" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="3575" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3576" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3576" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="3578" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3578" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="3580" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3582" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="3583" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3585" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3587" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#1636" class="Function">cong-ℕ</a> <a id="3594" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3595" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="3602" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3576" class="Bound">k</a><a id="3603" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3605" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3606" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="3614" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3615" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="3626" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3576" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="3628" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3578" class="Bound">x</a><a id="3629" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3632" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3578" class="Bound">x</a>
<a id="3634" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3551" class="Function">cong-nat-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="3654" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3654" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="3656" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1479" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕ</a> <a id="3663" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3665" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#4767" class="Function">cong-is-zero-nat-zero-Fin</a>
<a id="3691" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3551" class="Function">cong-nat-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="3711" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3711" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="3713" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3714" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="3721" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3721" class="Bound">x</a><a id="3722" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3724" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="3728" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#3148" class="Function">trans-cong-ℕ</a>
    <a id="3745" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="3747" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="3754" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3711" class="Bound">k</a><a id="3755" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="3761" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="3763" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="3771" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3772" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="3783" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3711" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="3785" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3786" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="3793" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3721" class="Bound">x</a><a id="3794" class="Symbol">)))</a>
    <a id="3802" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="3804" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="3811" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3812" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="3820" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3821" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="3832" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3711" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="3834" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3721" class="Bound">x</a><a id="3835" class="Symbol">)))</a>
    <a id="3843" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="3845" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="3852" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3721" class="Bound">x</a><a id="3853" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="3859" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="3861" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3082" class="Function">cong-nat-succ-Fin</a> <a id="3879" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3880" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="3887" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3711" class="Bound">k</a><a id="3888" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3890" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3891" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="3902" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3711" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="3904" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3721" class="Bound">x</a><a id="3905" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3907" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="3913" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="3915" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3551" class="Function">cong-nat-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="3935" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3711" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="3937" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3721" class="Bound">x</a><a id="3938" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
We show that if mod-succ-ℕ k x = mod-succ-ℕ k y, then x and y must be congruent modulo succ-ℕ n. This is the forward direction of the theorem.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="cong-eq-mod-succ-ℕ"></a><a id="4097" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4097" class="Function">cong-eq-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="4116" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="4120" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4121" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4121" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="4123" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4123" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4125" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4125" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="4127" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4129" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="4130" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4132" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4134" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="4145" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4121" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="4147" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4123" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4149" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="4151" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="4162" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4121" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="4164" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4125" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="4166" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4168" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#1636" class="Function">cong-ℕ</a> <a id="4175" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4176" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="4183" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4121" class="Bound">k</a><a id="4184" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4186" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4123" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4188" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4125" class="Bound">y</a>
<a id="4190" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4097" class="Function">cong-eq-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="4209" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4209" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="4211" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4211" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4213" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4213" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="4215" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4215" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="4217" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="4221" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#3644" class="Function">concatenate-cong-eq-cong-ℕ</a> <a id="4248" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4249" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="4256" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4209" class="Bound">k</a><a id="4257" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4259" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4260" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4211" class="Bound">x</a><a id="4261" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="4267" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="4269" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#2882" class="Function">symm-cong-ℕ</a> <a id="4281" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4282" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="4289" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4209" class="Bound">k</a><a id="4290" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4292" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4293" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="4301" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4302" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="4313" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4209" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="4315" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4211" class="Bound">x</a><a id="4316" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="4319" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4211" class="Bound">x</a>
      <a id="4327" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="4329" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3551" class="Function">cong-nat-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="4349" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4209" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="4351" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4211" class="Bound">x</a><a id="4352" class="Symbol">))</a>
    <a id="4359" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="4361" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="4364" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="4372" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4215" class="Bound">p</a><a id="4373" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="4379" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="4381" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3551" class="Function">cong-nat-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="4401" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4209" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="4403" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4213" class="Bound">y</a><a id="4404" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-zero-mod-succ-ℕ"></a><a id="4958" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4958" class="Function">is-zero-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="4977" class="Symbol">:</a>

<a id="5043" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4958" class="Function">is-zero-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="5062" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5062" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="5064" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5064" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="5066" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5066" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="5068" class="Symbol">=</a>

    <a id="5106" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5108" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers.html#2150" class="Function">concatenate-div-eq-ℕ</a> <a id="5129" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5066" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="5131" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5132" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="5136" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5137" href="elementary-number-theory.distance-natural-numbers.html#2735" class="Function">right-unit-law-dist-ℕ</a> <a id="5159" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5064" class="Bound">x</a><a id="5160" class="Symbol">)))</a>

<a id="div-is-zero-mod-succ-ℕ"></a><a id="5165" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5165" class="Function">div-is-zero-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="5188" class="Symbol">:</a>

<a id="5254" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5165" class="Function">div-is-zero-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="5277" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5277" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="5279" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5279" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="5281" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5281" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="5283" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="5287" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers.html#2150" class="Function">concatenate-div-eq-ℕ</a>
    <a id="5312" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5314" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4097" class="Function">cong-eq-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="5333" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5277" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="5335" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5279" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="5337" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1479" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕ</a> <a id="5344" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5281" class="Bound">p</a><a id="5345" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="5351" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5353" href="elementary-number-theory.distance-natural-numbers.html#2735" class="Function">right-unit-law-dist-ℕ</a> <a id="5375" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5279" class="Bound">x</a><a id="5376" class="Symbol">)</a>

### The inclusion of Fin k into ℕ is a section of mod-succ-ℕ

<pre class="Agda"><a id="issec-nat-Fin"></a><a id="5453" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5453" class="Function">issec-nat-Fin</a> <a id="5467" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="5471" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5472" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5472" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="5474" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5476" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="5477" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5479" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5480" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5480" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="5482" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5484" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="5488" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5489" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="5496" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5472" class="Bound">k</a><a id="5497" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5500" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5502" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="5513" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5472" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="5515" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5516" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="5524" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5480" class="Bound">x</a><a id="5525" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5527" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="5529" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5480" class="Bound">x</a>
<a id="5531" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5453" class="Function">issec-nat-Fin</a> <a id="5545" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5546" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5546" class="Bound">k</a><a id="5547" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5549" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5549" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="5551" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="5555" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#6359" class="Function">is-injective-nat-Fin</a>
    <a id="5580" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5582" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#4293" class="Function">eq-cong-le-ℕ</a>
      <a id="5601" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5603" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="5610" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5546" class="Bound">k</a><a id="5611" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="5619" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5621" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="5629" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5630" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="5641" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5546" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="5643" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5644" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="5652" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5549" class="Bound">x</a><a id="5653" class="Symbol">)))</a>
      <a id="5663" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5665" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="5673" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5549" class="Bound">x</a><a id="5674" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="5682" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5684" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5771" class="Function">strict-upper-bound-nat-Fin</a> <a id="5711" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5712" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="5723" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5546" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="5725" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5726" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="5734" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5549" class="Bound">x</a><a id="5735" class="Symbol">)))</a>
      <a id="5745" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5747" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5771" class="Function">strict-upper-bound-nat-Fin</a> <a id="5774" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5549" class="Bound">x</a><a id="5775" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="5783" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5785" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3551" class="Function">cong-nat-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="5805" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5546" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="5807" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5808" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="5816" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5549" class="Bound">x</a><a id="5817" class="Symbol">)))</a>

<a id="is-split-surjective-mod-succ-ℕ"></a><a id="5822" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5822" class="Function">is-split-surjective-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="5853" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="5857" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5858" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5858" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="5860" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5862" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="5863" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5865" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5867" href="foundation.split-surjective-maps.html#983" class="Function">is-split-surjective</a> <a id="5887" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5888" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="5899" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5858" class="Bound">k</a><a id="5900" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="5902" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="5906" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5907" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5822" class="Function">is-split-surjective-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="5938" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5939" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5939" class="Bound">k</a><a id="5940" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5942" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5942" class="Bound">x</a><a id="5943" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5945" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5947" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="5955" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5942" class="Bound">x</a>
<a id="5957" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="5961" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5962" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5822" class="Function">is-split-surjective-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="5993" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5994" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5994" class="Bound">k</a><a id="5995" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5997" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5997" class="Bound">x</a><a id="5998" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6000" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6002" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5453" class="Function">issec-nat-Fin</a> <a id="6016" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5997" class="Bound">x</a>
</pre>
## The group structure on the standard finite types

### Addition on finite sets

<pre class="Agda"><a id="add-Fin"></a><a id="6113" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6113" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="6121" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6123" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6124" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6124" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6126" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6128" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="6129" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6131" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6133" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="6137" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6124" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6139" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6141" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="6145" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6124" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6147" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6149" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="6153" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6124" class="Bound">k</a>
<a id="6155" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6113" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="6163" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6164" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="6171" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6171" class="Bound">k</a><a id="6172" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6174" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6174" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6176" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6176" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="6178" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6180" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="6191" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6171" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6193" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6194" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#1164" class="Function">add-ℕ</a> <a id="6200" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6201" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="6209" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6174" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6210" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6212" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6213" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="6221" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6176" class="Bound">y</a><a id="6222" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="add-Fin&#39;"></a><a id="6226" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6226" class="Function">add-Fin&#39;</a> <a id="6235" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6237" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6238" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6238" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6240" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6242" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="6243" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6245" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6247" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="6251" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6238" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6253" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6255" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="6259" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6238" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6261" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6263" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="6267" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6238" class="Bound">k</a>
<a id="6269" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6226" class="Function">add-Fin&#39;</a> <a id="6278" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6278" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6280" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6280" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="6282" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6284" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6113" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="6292" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6280" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="6294" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6278" class="Bound">x</a>

<a id="ap-add-Fin"></a><a id="6297" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6297" class="Function">ap-add-Fin</a> <a id="6308" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="6312" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6313" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6313" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6315" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6317" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="6318" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6320" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6321" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6321" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6323" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6323" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="6325" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6325" class="Bound">x&#39;</a> <a id="6328" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6328" class="Bound">y&#39;</a> <a id="6331" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6333" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="6337" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6313" class="Bound">k</a><a id="6338" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6340" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="6344" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6321" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6346" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="6348" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6325" class="Bound">x&#39;</a> <a id="6351" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6353" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6323" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="6355" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="6357" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6328" class="Bound">y&#39;</a> <a id="6360" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6362" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6113" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="6370" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6321" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6372" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6323" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="6374" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="6376" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6113" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="6384" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6325" class="Bound">x&#39;</a> <a id="6387" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6328" class="Bound">y&#39;</a>
<a id="6390" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6297" class="Function">ap-add-Fin</a> <a id="6401" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6401" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="6403" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6403" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="6405" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6407" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#7450" class="Function">ap-binary</a> <a id="6417" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6113" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="6425" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6401" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="6427" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6403" class="Bound">q</a>

  <a id="6447" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6448" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6448" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6450" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6452" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="6453" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6455" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6456" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6456" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6458" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6458" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="6460" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6462" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="6466" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6448" class="Bound">k</a><a id="6467" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6469" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="6473" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#1636" class="Function">cong-ℕ</a> <a id="6480" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6448" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6482" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6483" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="6491" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6492" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6113" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="6500" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6456" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6502" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6458" class="Bound">y</a><a id="6503" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="6506" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6507" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#1164" class="Function">add-ℕ</a> <a id="6513" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6514" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="6522" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6456" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6523" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6525" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6526" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="6534" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6458" class="Bound">y</a><a id="6535" class="Symbol">))</a>
<a id="6538" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6430" class="Function">cong-add-Fin</a> <a id="6551" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6552" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="6559" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6559" class="Bound">k</a><a id="6560" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6562" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6562" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6564" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6564" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="6566" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="6570" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3551" class="Function">cong-nat-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="6590" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6559" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6592" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6593" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#1164" class="Function">add-ℕ</a> <a id="6599" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6600" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="6608" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6562" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6609" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6611" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6612" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="6620" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6564" class="Bound">y</a><a id="6621" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="cong-add-ℕ"></a><a id="6625" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6625" class="Function">cong-add-ℕ</a> <a id="6636" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6638" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6639" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6639" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6641" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6643" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="6644" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6646" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6647" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6647" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6649" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6649" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="6651" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6653" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="6654" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6656" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="6660" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#1636" class="Function">cong-ℕ</a>
    <a id="6671" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6673" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="6680" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6639" class="Bound">k</a><a id="6681" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="6687" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6689" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#1164" class="Function">add-ℕ</a> <a id="6695" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6696" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="6704" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6705" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="6716" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6639" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6718" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6647" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6719" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="6722" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6723" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="6731" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6732" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="6743" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6639" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6745" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6649" class="Bound">y</a><a id="6746" class="Symbol">)))</a>
    <a id="6754" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6756" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#1164" class="Function">add-ℕ</a> <a id="6762" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6647" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6764" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6649" class="Bound">y</a><a id="6765" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="6767" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6625" class="Function">cong-add-ℕ</a> <a id="6778" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6779" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6779" class="Bound">k</a><a id="6780" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6782" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6782" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6784" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6784" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="6786" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="6790" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#3148" class="Function">trans-cong-ℕ</a> <a id="6803" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6804" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="6811" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6779" class="Bound">k</a><a id="6812" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="6818" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6820" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#1164" class="Function">add-ℕ</a> <a id="6826" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6827" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="6835" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6836" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="6847" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6779" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6849" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6782" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6850" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="6853" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6854" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="6862" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6863" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="6874" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6779" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6876" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6784" class="Bound">y</a><a id="6877" class="Symbol">)))</a>
    <a id="6885" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6887" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#1164" class="Function">add-ℕ</a> <a id="6893" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6782" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6895" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6896" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="6904" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6905" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="6916" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6779" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6918" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6784" class="Bound">y</a><a id="6919" class="Symbol">)))</a>
    <a id="6927" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6929" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#1164" class="Function">add-ℕ</a> <a id="6935" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6782" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6937" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6784" class="Bound">y</a><a id="6938" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="6944" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6946" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#6597" class="Function">translation-invariant-cong-ℕ&#39;</a>
      <a id="6982" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6984" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="6991" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6779" class="Bound">k</a><a id="6992" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="7000" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7002" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="7010" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7011" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="7022" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6779" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7024" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6782" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7025" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="7034" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7036" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6782" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7037" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="7045" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7047" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="7055" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7056" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="7067" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6779" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7069" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6784" class="Bound">y</a><a id="7070" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="7079" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7081" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3551" class="Function">cong-nat-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="7101" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6779" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7103" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6782" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7104" class="Symbol">))</a>
    <a id="7111" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7113" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#6338" class="Function">translation-invariant-cong-ℕ</a>
      <a id="7148" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7150" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="7157" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6779" class="Bound">k</a><a id="7158" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="7166" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7168" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="7176" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7177" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="7188" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6779" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7190" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6784" class="Bound">y</a><a id="7191" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="7200" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7202" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6784" class="Bound">y</a><a id="7203" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="7211" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7213" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6782" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7214" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="7222" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7224" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3551" class="Function">cong-nat-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="7244" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6779" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7246" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6784" class="Bound">y</a><a id="7247" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
### Distance on finite sets

<pre class="Agda"><a id="dist-Fin"></a><a id="7292" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7292" class="Function">dist-Fin</a> <a id="7301" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7303" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7304" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7304" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7306" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7308" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="7309" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7311" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7313" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="7317" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7304" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7319" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7321" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="7325" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7304" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7327" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7329" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="7333" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7304" class="Bound">k</a>
<a id="7335" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7292" class="Function">dist-Fin</a> <a id="7344" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7345" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="7352" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7352" class="Bound">k</a><a id="7353" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7355" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7355" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7357" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7357" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="7359" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7361" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="7372" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7352" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7374" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7375" href="elementary-number-theory.distance-natural-numbers.html#1255" class="Function">dist-ℕ</a> <a id="7382" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7383" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="7391" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7355" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7392" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7394" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7395" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="7403" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7357" class="Bound">y</a><a id="7404" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="dist-Fin&#39;"></a><a id="7408" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7408" class="Function">dist-Fin&#39;</a> <a id="7418" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7420" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7421" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7421" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7423" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7425" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="7426" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7428" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7430" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="7434" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7421" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7436" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7438" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="7442" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7421" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7444" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7446" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="7450" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7421" class="Bound">k</a>
<a id="7452" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7408" class="Function">dist-Fin&#39;</a> <a id="7462" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7462" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7464" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7464" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="7466" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7468" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7292" class="Function">dist-Fin</a> <a id="7477" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7464" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="7479" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7462" class="Bound">x</a>

<a id="ap-dist-Fin"></a><a id="7482" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7482" class="Function">ap-dist-Fin</a> <a id="7494" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="7498" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7499" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7499" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7501" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7503" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="7504" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7506" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7507" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7507" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7509" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7509" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="7511" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7511" class="Bound">x&#39;</a> <a id="7514" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7514" class="Bound">y&#39;</a> <a id="7517" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7519" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="7523" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7499" class="Bound">k</a><a id="7524" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7526" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="7530" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7507" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7532" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="7534" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7511" class="Bound">x&#39;</a> <a id="7537" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7539" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7509" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="7541" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="7543" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7514" class="Bound">y&#39;</a> <a id="7546" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7548" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7292" class="Function">dist-Fin</a> <a id="7557" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7507" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7559" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7509" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="7561" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="7563" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7292" class="Function">dist-Fin</a> <a id="7572" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7511" class="Bound">x&#39;</a> <a id="7575" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7514" class="Bound">y&#39;</a>
<a id="7578" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7482" class="Function">ap-dist-Fin</a> <a id="7590" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7590" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="7592" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7592" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="7594" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7596" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#7450" class="Function">ap-binary</a> <a id="7606" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7292" class="Function">dist-Fin</a> <a id="7615" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7590" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="7617" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7592" class="Bound">q</a>

<a id="cong-dist-Fin"></a><a id="7620" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7620" class="Function">cong-dist-Fin</a> <a id="7634" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="7638" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7639" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7639" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7641" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7643" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="7644" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7646" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7647" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7647" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7649" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7649" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="7651" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7653" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="7657" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7639" class="Bound">k</a><a id="7658" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7660" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="7664" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#1636" class="Function">cong-ℕ</a> <a id="7671" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7639" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7673" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7674" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="7682" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7683" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7292" class="Function">dist-Fin</a> <a id="7692" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7647" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7694" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7649" class="Bound">y</a><a id="7695" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="7698" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7699" href="elementary-number-theory.distance-natural-numbers.html#1255" class="Function">dist-ℕ</a> <a id="7706" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7707" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="7715" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7647" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7716" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7718" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7719" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="7727" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7649" class="Bound">y</a><a id="7728" class="Symbol">))</a>
<a id="7731" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7620" class="Function">cong-dist-Fin</a> <a id="7745" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7746" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="7753" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7753" class="Bound">k</a><a id="7754" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7756" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7756" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7758" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7758" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="7760" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="7764" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3551" class="Function">cong-nat-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="7784" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7753" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7786" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7787" href="elementary-number-theory.distance-natural-numbers.html#1255" class="Function">dist-ℕ</a> <a id="7794" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7795" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="7803" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7756" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7804" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7806" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7807" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="7815" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7758" class="Bound">y</a><a id="7816" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
### The negative of an element of Fin k

<pre class="Agda"><a id="neg-Fin"></a><a id="7873" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7873" class="Function">neg-Fin</a> <a id="7881" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="7885" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7886" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7886" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7888" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7890" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="7891" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7893" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7895" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="7899" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7886" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7901" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7903" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="7907" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7886" class="Bound">k</a>
<a id="7909" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7873" class="Function">neg-Fin</a> <a id="7917" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7918" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="7925" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7925" class="Bound">k</a><a id="7926" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7928" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7928" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7930" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="7934" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="7945" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7925" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7947" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7948" href="elementary-number-theory.distance-natural-numbers.html#1255" class="Function">dist-ℕ</a> <a id="7955" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7956" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="7964" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7928" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7965" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7967" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7968" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="7975" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7925" class="Bound">k</a><a id="7976" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="cong-neg-Fin"></a><a id="7980" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7980" class="Function">cong-neg-Fin</a> <a id="7993" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="7997" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7998" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7998" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8000" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8002" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="8003" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8005" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8006" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8006" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8008" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8010" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="8014" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7998" class="Bound">k</a><a id="8015" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8017" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="8021" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#1636" class="Function">cong-ℕ</a> <a id="8028" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7998" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8030" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8031" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="8039" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8040" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7873" class="Function">neg-Fin</a> <a id="8048" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8006" class="Bound">x</a><a id="8049" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="8052" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8053" href="elementary-number-theory.distance-natural-numbers.html#1255" class="Function">dist-ℕ</a> <a id="8060" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8061" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="8069" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8006" class="Bound">x</a><a id="8070" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8072" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7998" class="Bound">k</a><a id="8073" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="8075" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7980" class="Function">cong-neg-Fin</a> <a id="8088" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8089" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="8096" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8096" class="Bound">k</a><a id="8097" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8099" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8099" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8101" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="8105" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3551" class="Function">cong-nat-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="8125" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8096" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8127" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8128" href="elementary-number-theory.distance-natural-numbers.html#1255" class="Function">dist-ℕ</a> <a id="8135" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8136" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="8144" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8099" class="Bound">x</a><a id="8145" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8147" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8148" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="8155" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8096" class="Bound">k</a><a id="8156" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
<pre class="Agda"><a id="congruence-add-ℕ"></a><a id="8172" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8172" class="Function">congruence-add-ℕ</a> <a id="8189" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="8193" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8194" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8194" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8196" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8198" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="8199" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8201" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8202" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8202" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8204" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8204" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="8206" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8206" class="Bound">x&#39;</a> <a id="8209" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8209" class="Bound">y&#39;</a> <a id="8212" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8214" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="8215" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8217" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="8221" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#1636" class="Function">cong-ℕ</a> <a id="8228" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8194" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8230" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8202" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8232" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8206" class="Bound">x&#39;</a> <a id="8235" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8237" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#1636" class="Function">cong-ℕ</a> <a id="8244" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8194" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8246" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8204" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="8248" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8262" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8263" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#1164" class="Function">add-ℕ</a> <a id="8269" class="Bound">y</a><a id="8272" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8274" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8275" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#1164" class="Function">add-ℕ</a> <a
