<a id="8288" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8172" class="Function">congruence-add-ℕ</a> <a id="8305" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8305" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8307" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8308" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8308" class="Bound">x</a><a id="8309" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8311" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8312" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8312" class="Bound">y</a><a id="8313" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8315" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8316" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8316" class="Bound">x&#39;</a><a id="8318" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8320" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8321" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8321" class="Bound">y&#39;</a><a id="8323" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8325" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8325" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="8327" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8327" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="8329" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="8333" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#3148" class="Function">trans-cong-ℕ</a> <a id="8346" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8305" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8348" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8349" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#1164" class="Function">add-ℕ</a> <a id="8355" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8308" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8357" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8312" class="Bound">y</a><a id="8358" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8360" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8361" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#1164" class="Function">add-ℕ</a> <a id="8367" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8308" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8369" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8321" class="Bound">y&#39;</a><a id="8371" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8373" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8374" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#1164" class="Function">add-ℕ</a> <a id="8380" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8316" class="Bound">x&#39;</a> <a id="8383" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8321" class="Bound">y&#39;</a><a id="8385" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="8391" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8393" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#6338" class="Function">translation-invariant-cong-ℕ</a> <a id="8422" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8305" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8424" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8312" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="8426" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8321" class="Bound">y&#39;</a> <a id="8429" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8308" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8431" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8327" class="Bound">K</a><a id="8432" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="8438" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8440" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#6597" class="Function">translation-invariant-cong-ℕ&#39;</a> <a id="8470" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8305" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8472" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8308" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8474" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8316" class="Bound">x&#39;</a> <a id="8477" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8321" class="Bound">y&#39;</a> <a id="8480" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8325" class="Bound">H</a><a id="8481" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="mod-succ-add-ℕ"></a><a id="8484" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8484" class="Function">mod-succ-add-ℕ</a> <a id="8499" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="8503" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8504" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8504" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8506" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8506" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8508" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8508" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="8510" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8512" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="8513" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8515" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="8519" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="8530" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8504" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8532" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8533" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#1164" class="Function">add-ℕ</a> <a id="8539" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8506" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8541" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8508" class="Bound">y</a><a id="8542" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8544" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="8546" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6113" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="8554" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8555" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="8566" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8504" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8568" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8506" class="Bound">x</a><a id="8569" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8571" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8572" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="8583" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8504" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8585" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8508" class="Bound">y</a><a id="8586" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="8588" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8484" class="Function">mod-succ-add-ℕ</a> <a id="8603" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8603" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8605" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8605" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8607" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8607" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="8609" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="8613" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4419" class="Function">eq-mod-succ-cong-ℕ</a> <a id="8632" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8603" class="Bound">k</a>
    <a id="8638" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8640" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#1164" class="Function">add-ℕ</a> <a id="8646" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8605" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8648" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8607" class="Bound">y</a><a id="8649" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="8655" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8657" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#1164" class="Function">add-ℕ</a> <a id="8663" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8664" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="8672" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8673" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="8684" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8603" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8686" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8605" class="Bound">x</a><a id="8687" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="8690" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8691" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="8699" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8700" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="8711" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8603" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8713" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8607" class="Bound">y</a><a id="8714" class="Symbol">)))</a>
    <a id="8722" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8724" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8172" class="Function">congruence-add-ℕ</a>
      <a id="8747" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8749" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="8756" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8603" class="Bound">k</a><a id="8757" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="8765" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="8767" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8605" class="Bound">x</a><a id="8768" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="8776" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="8778" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8607" class="Bound">y</a><a id="8779" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="8787" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="8789" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="8797" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8798" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="8809" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8603" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8811" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8605" class="Bound">x</a><a id="8812" class="Symbol">)}</a>
      <a id="8821" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="8823" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="8831" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8832" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="8843" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8603" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8845" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8607" class="Bound">y</a><a id="8846" class="Symbol">)}</a>
      <a id="8855" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8857" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#2882" class="Function">symm-cong-ℕ</a> <a id="8869" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8870" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="8877" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8603" class="Bound">k</a><a id="8878" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8880" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8881" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="8889" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8890" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="8901" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8603" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8903" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8605" class="Bound">x</a><a id="8904" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="8907" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8605" class="Bound">x</a>
        <a id="8917" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8919" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3551" class="Function">cong-nat-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="8939" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8603" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8941" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8605" class="Bound">x</a><a id="8942" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="8951" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8953" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#2882" class="Function">symm-cong-ℕ</a> <a id="8965" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8966" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="8973" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8603" class="Bound">k</a><a id="8974" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8976" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8977" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="8985" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8986" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="8997" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8603" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8999" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8607" class="Bound">y</a><a id="9000" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="9003" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8607" class="Bound">y</a>
        <a id="9013" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="9015" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3551" class="Function">cong-nat-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="9035" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8603" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="9037" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8607" class="Bound">y</a><a id="9038" class="Symbol">)))</a>
</pre>
## Laws for addition on Fin k

<pre class="Agda"><a id="commutative-add-Fin"></a><a id="9086" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#9086" class="Function">commutative-add-Fin</a> <a id="9106" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9108" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9109" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#9109" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="9111" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9113" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="9114" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9116" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9117" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#9117" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9119" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#9119" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="9121" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9123" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="9127" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#9109" class="Bound">k</a><a id="9128" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9130" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9132" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6113" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="9140" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#9117" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9142" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#9119" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="9144" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="9146" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6113" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="9154" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#9119" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="9156" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#9117" class="Bound">x</a>
<a id="9158" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#9086" class="Function">commutative-add-Fin</a> <a id="9178" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9179" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="9186" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#9186" class="Bound">k</a><a id="9187" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9189" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#9189" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9191" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#9191" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="9193" class="Symbol">=</a>

<a id="is-add-one-succ-Fin"></a><a id="12430" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12430" class="Function">is-add-one-succ-Fin</a> <a id="12450" class="Symbol">:</a>

<a id="12516" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12430" class="Function">is-add-one-succ-Fin</a> <a id="12536" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12536" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="12538" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12540" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12110" class="Function">is-add-one-succ-Fin&#39;</a> <a id="12561" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12536" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="12563" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a> <a id="12565" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#9086" class="Function">commutative-add-Fin</a> <a id="12585" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12536" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="12587" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#8398" class="Function">one-Fin</a>

<a id="right-successor-law-add-Fin"></a><a id="12653" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12653" class="Function">right-successor-law-add-Fin</a> <a id="12681" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="12685" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12686" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12686" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="12688" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12690" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="12691" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12693" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12694" class="Bound">k</a><a id="12705" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12707" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12709" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6113" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="12717" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12694" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="12719" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12720" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7668" class="Function">succ-Fin</a> <a id="12729" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12696" class="Bound">y</a><a id="12730" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12732" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="12734" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7668" class="Function">succ-Fin</a> <a id="12743" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12744" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6113" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="12752" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12694" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="12754" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12696" class="Bound">y</a><a id="12755" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="12757" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12653" class="Function">right-successor-law-add-Fin</a> <a id="12785" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12786" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="12793" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12793" class="Bound">k</a><a id="12794" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12796" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12796" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="12798" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12798" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="12800" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="12804" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12806" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="12809" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12810" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6113" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="12818" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12796" class="Bound">x</a><a id="12819" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12821" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12822" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12110" class="Function">is-add-one-succ-Fin&#39;</a> <a id="12843" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12798" class="Bound">y</a><a id="12844" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="12847" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
  <a id="12851" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12853" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12855" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="12859" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12860" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#9260" class="Function">associative-add-Fin</a> <a id="12880" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12796" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="12882" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12798" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="12884" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#8398" class="Function">one-Fin</a><a id="12891" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="12894" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
    <a id="12900" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12902" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="12906" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12907" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12110" class="Function">is-add-one-succ-Fin&#39;</a> <a id="12928" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12929" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6113" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="12937" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12796" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="12939" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12798" class="Bound">y</a><a id="12940" class="Symbol">))))</a>

<a id="left-successor-law-add-Fin"></a><a id="12946" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12946" class="Function">left-successor-law-add-Fin</a> <a id="12973" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="12977" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12978" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12978" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="12980" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12982" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="12983" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12985" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12986" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12986" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="12988" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12988" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="12990" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12992" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="12996" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12978" class="Bound">k</a><a id="12997" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12999" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13001" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6113" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="13009" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13010" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7668" class="Function">succ-Fin</a> <a id="13019" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12986" class="Bound">x</a><a id="13020" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13022" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12988" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="13024" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="13026" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7668" class="Function">succ-Fin</a> <a id="13035" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13036" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6113" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="13044" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12986" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13046" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12988" class="Bound">y</a><a id="13047" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="13049" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12946" class="Function">left-successor-law-add-Fin</a> <a id="13076" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13076" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13078" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13078" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="13080" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="13084" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#9086" class="Function">commutative-add-Fin</a> <a id="13104" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13105" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7668" class="Function">succ-Fin</a> <a id="13114" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13076" class="Bound">x</a><a id="13115" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13117" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13078" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="13119" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
  <a id="13123" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="13125" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="13127" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12653" class="Function">right-successor-law-add-Fin</a> <a id="13155" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13078" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="13157" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13076" class="Bound">x</a><a id="13158" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13160" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
    <a id="13166" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="13168" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="13171" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7668" class="Function">succ-Fin</a> <a id="13180" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13181" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#9086" class="Function">commutative-add-Fin</a> <a id="13201" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13078" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="13203" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13076" class="Bound">x</a><a id="13204" class="Symbol">)))</a>
</pre>
## Multiplication on Fin k

<pre class="Agda"><a id="13249" class="Comment">{- We define the multiplication on the types Fin k. -}</a>

  <a id="13317" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13318" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13318" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="13320" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13322" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="13323" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13325" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13327" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="13331" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13318" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="13333" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13335" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="13339" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13318" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="13341" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13343" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="13347" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13318" class="Bound">k</a>
<a id="13349" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13305" class="Function">mul-Fin</a> <a id="13357" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13358" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="13365" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13365" class="Bound">k</a><a id="13366" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13368" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13368" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13370" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13370" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="13372" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13374" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="13385" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13365" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="13387" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13388" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers.html#1358" class="Function">mul-ℕ</a> <a id="13394" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13395" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="13403" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13368" class="Bound">x</a><a id="13404" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13406" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13407" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="13415" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13370" class="Bound">y</a><a id="13416" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="mul-Fin&#39;"></a><a id="13420" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13420" class="Function">mul-Fin&#39;</a> <a id="13429" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="13433" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13434" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13434" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="13436" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13438" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="13439" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13441" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13443" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="13447" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13434" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="13449" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13451" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="13455" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13434" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="13457" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13459" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="13463" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13434" class="Bound">k</a>
<a id="13465" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13420" class="Function">mul-Fin&#39;</a> <a id="13474" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13475" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13475" class="Bound">k</a><a id="13476" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13478" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13478" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13480" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13480" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="13482" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13484" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13305" class="Function">mul-Fin</a> <a id="13492" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13480" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="13494" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13478" class="Bound">x</a>

  <a id="13512" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13513" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13513" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="13515" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13574" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13305" class="Function">mul-Fin</a> <a id="13582" <a id="13588" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13497" class="Function">ap-mul-Fin</a> <a id="13599" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13599" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="13601" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13601" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="13603" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13605" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#7450" class="Function">ap-binary</a> <a id="13615" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13305" class="Function">mul-Fin</a> <a id="13623" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13599" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="13625" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13601" class="Bound">q</a>

<a id="cong-mul-Fin"></a><a id="13628" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13628" class="Function">cong-mul-Fin</a> <a id="13641" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="13645" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13646" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13646" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="13648" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13650" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="13651" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13653" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13654" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13654" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13656" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13656" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="13658" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13660" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="13664" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13646" class="Bound">k</a><a id="13665" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13667" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="13671" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#1636" class="Function">cong-ℕ</a> <a id="13678" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13646" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="13680" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13681" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="13689" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13690" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13305" class="Function">mul-Fin</a> <a id="13698" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13654" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13700" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13656" class="Bound">y</a><a id="13701" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="13704" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13705" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers.html#1358" class="Function">mul-ℕ</a> <a id="13711" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13712" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="13720" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13654" class="Bound">x</a><a id="13721" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13723" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13724" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="13732" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13656" class="Bound">y</a><a id="13733" class="Symbol">))</a>
<a id="13736" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13628" class="Function">cong-mul-Fin</a> <a id="13749" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13750" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="13757" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13757" class="Bound">k</a><a id="13758" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13760" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13760" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13762" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13762" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="13764" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="13768" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#3551" class="Function">cong-nat-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="13788" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13757" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="13790" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13791" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers.html#1358" class="Function">mul-ℕ</a> <a id="13797" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13798" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="13806" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13760" class="Bound">x</a><a id="13807" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13809" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13810" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="13818" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13762" class="Bound">y</a><a id="13819" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
## Laws for multiplication on the standard finite types

<pre class="Agda"><a id="associative-mul-Fin"></a><a id="13892" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13892" class="Function">associative-mul-Fin</a> <a id="13912" class="Symbol">:</a>

<a id="commutative-mul-Fin"></a><a id="15023" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#15023" class="Function">commutative-mul-Fin</a> <a id="15043" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="15047" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15048" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#15048" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="15050" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15052" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="15053" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15055" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15056" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#15056" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15058" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#15058" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="15060" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15062" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="15066" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#15048" class="Bound">k</a><a id="15067" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15069" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15071" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13305" class="Function">mul-Fin</a> <a id="15079" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#15056" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15081" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#15058" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="15083" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="15085" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13305" class="Function">mul-Fin</a> <a id="15093" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#15058" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="15095" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#15056" class="Bound">x</a>
<a id="15097" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#15023" class="Function">commutative-mul-Fin</a> <a id="15117" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15118" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="15125" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#15125" class="Bound">k</a><a id="15126" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15128" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#15128" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15130" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#15130" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="15132" class="Symbol">=</a>

      <a id="16302" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="16304" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="16312" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16313" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7083" class="Function">zero-Fin</a> <a id="16322" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16323" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16086" class="Bound">k</a><a id="16324" class="Symbol">})}</a>
      <a id="16334" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16336" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16338" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="16341" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16342" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers.html#1432" class="Function">mul-ℕ&#39;</a> <a id="16349" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16350" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="16358" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16089" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16359" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="16362" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16363" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7884" class="Function">is-zero-nat-zero-Fin</a> <a id="16384" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16385" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16086" class="Bound">k</a><a id="16386" class="Symbol">}))</a> <a id="16390" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
        <a id="16400" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16402" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="16406" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16407" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7884" class="Function">is-zero-nat-zero-Fin</a> <a id="16428" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16429" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16086" class="Bound">k</a><a id="16430" class="Symbol">})))))</a> <a id="16437" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
  <a id="16441" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16443" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5453" class="Function">issec-nat-Fin</a> <a id="16457" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16458" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7083" class="Function">zero-Fin</a> <a id="16467" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16468" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16086" class="Bound">k</a><a id="16469" class="Symbol">}))</a>

<a id="right-zero-law-mul-Fin"></a><a id="16474" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16474" class="Function">right-zero-law-mul-Fin</a> <a id="16497" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="16501" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16502" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16502" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="16504" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16506" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="16507" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16509" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16510" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16510" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16512" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16514" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="16518" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16519" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="16526" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16502" class="Bound">k</a><a id="16527" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="16530" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16532" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13305" class="Function">mul-Fin</a> <a id="16540" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16510" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16542" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7083" class="Function">zero-Fin</a> <a id="16551" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="16553" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7083" class="Function">zero-Fin</a>
<a id="16562" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16474" class="Function">right-zero-law-mul-Fin</a> <a id="16585" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16585" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16587" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="16591" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16593" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#15023" class="Function">commutative-mul-Fin</a> <a id="16613" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16585" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16615" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7083" class="Function">zero-Fin</a><a id="16623" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16625" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
  <a id="16629" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16631" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#15976" class="Function">left-zero-law-mul-Fin</a> <a id="16653" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16585" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16654" class="Symbol">)</a>

        <a id="17500" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17502" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#2602" class="Function">refl-cong-ℕ</a> <a id="17514" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17515" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="17522" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16819" class="Bound">k</a><a id="17523" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17525" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17526" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="17534" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16822" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17535" class="Symbol">))</a>

      <a id="17573" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17575" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers.html#3446" class="Function">left-distributive-mul-add-ℕ</a> <a id="17603" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17604" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="17612" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16822" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17613" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17615" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17616" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="17624" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16824" class="Bound">y</a><a id="17625" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17627" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17628" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="17636" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16826" class="Bound">z</a><a id="17637" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="17646" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17648" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers.html#2882" class="Function">symm-cong-ℕ</a> <a id="17660" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17661" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="17668" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16819" class="Bound">k</a><a id="17669" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="17679" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17681" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#1164" class="Function">add-ℕ</a> <a id="17687" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17689" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="17697" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17698" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13305" class="Function">mul-Fin</a> <a id="17706" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16822" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="17708" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16824" class="Bound">y</a><a id="17709" class="Symbol">))</a>
                <a id="17728" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17730" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="17738" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17739" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13305" class="Function">mul-Fin</a> <a id="17747" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16822" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="17749" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16826" class="Bound">z</a><a id="17750" class="Symbol">)))</a>
        <a id="17762" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17764" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#1164" class="Function">add-ℕ</a> <a id="17770" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17772" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers.html#1358" class="Function">mul-ℕ</a> <a id="17778" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17779" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="17787" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16822" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17788" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17790" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17791" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="17799" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16824" class="Bound">y</a><a id="17800" class="Symbol">))</a>
                <a id="17819" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17821" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers.html#1358" class="Function">mul-ℕ</a> <a id="17827" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17828" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="17836" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16822" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17837" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17839" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17840" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="17848" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16826" class="Bound">z</a><a id="17849" class="Symbol">)))</a>
        <a id="17861" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17863" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#8172" class="Function">congruence-add-ℕ</a>
          <a id="17890" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17892" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="17899" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16819" class="Bound">k</a><a id="17900" class="Symbol">)</a>
          <a id="17912" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="17914" class="Argument">x</a> <a id="17916" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17918" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="17926" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17927" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13305" class="Function">mul-Fin</a> <a id="17935" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16822" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="17937" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16824" class="Bound">y</a><a id="17938" class="Symbol">)}</a>
          <a id="17951" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="17953" class="Argument">y</a> <a id="17955" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17957" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="17965" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17966" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13305" class="Function">mul-Fin</a> <a id="17974" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16822" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="17976" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16826" class="Bound">z</a><a id="17977" class="Symbol">)}</a>
          <a id="17990" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="17992" class="Argument">x&#39;</a> <a id="17995" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17997" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers.html#1358" class="Function">mul-ℕ</a> <a id="18003" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18004" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="18012" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16822" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18013" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18015" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18016" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="18024" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16824" class="Bound">y</a><a id="18025" class="Symbol">)}</a>
          <a id="18038" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="18040" class="Argument">y&#39;</a> <a id="18043" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18045" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers.html#1358" class="Function">mul-ℕ</a> <a id="18051" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18052" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="18060" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16822" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18061" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18063" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18064" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#5670" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="18072" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16826" class="Bound">z</a><a id="18073" class="Symbol">)}</a>
          <a id="18086" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18088" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13628" class="Function">cong-mul-Fin</a> <a id="18101" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16822" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18103" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16824" class="Bound">y</a><a id="18104" class="Symbol">)</a>
          <a id="18116" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18118" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13628" class="Function">cong-mul-Fin</a> <a id="18131" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16822" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18133" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16826" class="Bound">z</a><a id="18134" class="Symbol">))))</a>

<a id="right-distributive-mul-add-Fin"></a><a id="18140" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18140" class="Function">right-distributive-mul-add-Fin</a> <a id="18171" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="18175" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18176" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18176" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="18178" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18180" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="18181" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18183" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18184" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18184" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18186" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18186" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="18188" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18188" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="18190" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18192" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="18196" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18176" class="Bound">k</a><a id="18197" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18199" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="18203" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13305" class="Function">mul-Fin</a> <a id="18211" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18212" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6113" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="18220" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18184" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18222" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18186" class="Bound">y</a><a id="18223" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18225" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18188" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="18227" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="18229" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6113" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="18237" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18238" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13305" class="Function">mul-Fin</a> <a id="18246" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18184" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18248" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18188" class="Bound">z</a><a id="18249" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18251" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18252" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13305" class="Function">mul-Fin</a> <a id="18260" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18186" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="18262" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18188" class="Bound">z</a><a id="18263" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="18265" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18140" class="Function">right-distributive-mul-add-Fin</a> <a id="18296" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18297" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18297" class="Bound">k</a><a id="18298" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18300" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18300" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18302" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18302" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="18304" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18304" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="18306" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="18310" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18312" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#15023" class="Function">commutative-mul-Fin</a> <a id="18332" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18333" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6113" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="18341" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18300" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18343" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18302" class="Bound">y</a><a id="18344" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18346" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18304" class="Bound">z</a><a id="18347" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18349" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
  <a id="18353" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18355" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18357" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16657" class="Function">left-distributive-mul-add-Fin</a> <a id="18387" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18304" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="18389" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18300" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18391" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18302" class="Bound">y</a><a id="18392" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18394" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
    <a id="18400" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18402" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6297" class="Function">ap-add-Fin</a> <a id="18413" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18414" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#15023" class="Function">commutative-mul-Fin</a> <a id="18434" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18304" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="18436" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18300" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18437" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18439" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18440" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#15023" class="Function">commutative-mul-Fin</a> <a id="18460" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18304" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="18462" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18302" class="Bound">y</a><a id="18463" class="Symbol">)))</a>
</pre>
<pre class="Agda"><a id="add-add-neg-Fin"></a><a id="18480" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18480" class="Function">add-add-neg-Fin</a> <a id="18496" class="Symbol">:</a>

<a id="18562" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18480" class="Function">add-add-neg-Fin</a> <a id="18578" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18579" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="18586" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18586" class="Bound">k</a><a id="18587" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18589" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18589" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18591" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18591" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="18593" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="18597" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18599" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="18603" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18604" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#9260" class="Function">associative-add-Fin</a> <a id="18624" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18589" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18626" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18627" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7873" class="Function">neg-Fin</a> <a id="18635" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18589" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18636" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18638" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18591" class="Bound">y</a><a id="18639" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18642" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
  <a id="18646" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18648" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18650" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="18653" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18654" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6226" class="Function">add-Fin&#39;</a> <a id="18663" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18591" class="Bound">y</a><a id="18664" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18666" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18667" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#11900" class="Function">right-inverse-law-add-Fin</a> <a id="18693" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18589" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18694" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18697" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
    <a id="18703" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18705" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#10998" class="Function">left-unit-law-add-Fin</a> <a id="18727" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18591" class="Bound">y</a><a id="18728" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="add-neg-add-Fin"></a><a id="18732" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18732" class="Function">add-neg-add-Fin</a> <a id="18748" class="Symbol">:</a>

  <a id="19801" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19803" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19805" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="19808" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19809" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6113" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="19817" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#19752" class="Bound">y</a><a id="19818" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19820" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19821" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#11900" class="Function">right-inverse-law-add-Fin</a> <a id="19847" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#19750" class="Bound">x</a><a id="19848" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="19851" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>

  <a id="20420" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20422" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="20426" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20427" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18732" class="Function">add-neg-add-Fin</a> <a id="20443" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#20404" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="20445" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#20407" class="Bound">y</a><a id="20446" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="20449" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>

<pre class="Agda"><a id="mul-neg-one-Fin"></a><a id="20730" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#20730" class="Function">mul-neg-one-Fin</a> <a id="20746" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="20750" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20751" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#20751" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="20753" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20755" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="20756" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20758" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20759" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#20759" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="20761" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20763" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="20767" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20768" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="20775" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#20751" class="Bound">k</a><a id="20776" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="20779" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20781" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13305" class="Function">mul-Fin</a> <a id="20789" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2413" class="Function">neg-one-Fin</a> <a id="20801" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#20759" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="20803" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="20805" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7873" class="Function">neg-Fin</a> <a id="20813" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#20759" class="Bound">x</a>
<a id="20815" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#20730" class="Function">mul-neg-one-Fin</a> <a id="20831" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20832" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#20832" class="Bound">k</a><a id="20833" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20835" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#20835" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="20837" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="20841" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#20307" class="Function">is-injective-add-Fin</a> <a id="20862" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#20835" class="Bound">x</a>
    <a id="20868" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20870" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20872" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20874" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a>
          <a id="20887" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20889" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6226" class="Function">add-Fin&#39;</a> <a id="20898" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20899" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13305" class="Function">mul-Fin</a> <a id="20907" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2413" class="Function">neg-one-Fin</a> <a id="20919" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#20835" class="Bound">x</a><a id="20920" class="Symbol">))</a>
          <a id="20933" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20935" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="20939" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20940" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#15330" class="Function">left-unit-law-mul-Fin</a> <a id="20962" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#20835" class="Bound">x</a><a id="20963" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="20967" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
        <a id="20977" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20979" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20981" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="20985" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20986" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#18140" class="Function">right-distributive-mul-add-Fin</a> <a id="21017" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#8398" class="Function">one-Fin</a> <a id="21025" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2413" class="Function">neg-one-Fin</a> <a id="21037" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#20835" class="Bound">x</a><a id="21038" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="21041" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>

      <a id="21166" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="21168" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="21172" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21173" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#11900" class="Function">right-inverse-law-add-Fin</a> <a id="21199" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#20835" class="Bound">x</a><a id="21200" class="Symbol">)))</a>

    <a id="25304" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="25306" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="25310" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25311" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#21766" class="Function">is-add-neg-one-pred-Fin&#39;</a> <a id="25336" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25337" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6113" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="25345" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#25192" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="25347" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#25194" class="Bound">y</a><a id="25348" class="Symbol">))))</a>

<a id="26338" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#26231" class="Function">right-successor-law-mul-Fin</a> <a id="26366" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26367" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="26374" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#26374" class="Bound">k</a><a id="26375" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26377" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#26377" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="26379" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#26379" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="26381" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="26385" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="26387" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="26390" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26391" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#13305" class="Function">mul-Fin</a> <a id="26399" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#26377" class="Bound">x</a><a id="26400" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="26402" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26403" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#12430" class="Function">is-add-one-succ-Fin</a> <a id="26423" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#26379" class="Bound">y</a><a id="26424" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="26427" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
  <a id="26431" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="26433" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="26435" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#16657" class="Function">left-distributive-mul-add-Fin</a> <a id="26465" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#26377" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="26467" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#8398" class="Function">one-Fin</a> <a id="26475" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#26379" class="Bound">y</a><a id="26476" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="26478" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>

<a id="27309" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27239" class="Function">leq-nat-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="27328" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27328" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="27330" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1479" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕ</a> <a id="27337" class="Symbol">=</a>
