</pre>
## Decidability of division

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-decidable-div-ℕ"></a><a id="27691" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27691" class="Function">is-decidable-div-ℕ</a> <a id="27710" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27712" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27713" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27713" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="27715" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27715" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="27717" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27719" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="27720" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27722" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27724" href="foundation.decidable-types.html#1918" class="Function">is-decidable</a> <a id="27737" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27738" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers.html#1608" class="Function">div-ℕ</a> <a id="27744" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27713" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="27746" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27715" class="Bound">x</a><a id="27747" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="27749" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27691" class="Function">is-decidable-div-ℕ</a> <a id="27768" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1479" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕ</a> <a id="27775" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27775" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="27777" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="27781" href="foundation.decidable-types.html#5063" class="Function">is-decidable-iff</a>
    <a id="27802" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27804" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers.html#8132" class="Function">div-eq-ℕ</a> <a id="27813" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1479" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕ</a> <a id="27820" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27775" class="Bound">x</a><a id="27821" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="27827" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27829" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="27833" href="foundation-core.functions.html#420" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="27835" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27836" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers.html#7599" class="Function">is-zero-div-zero-ℕ</a> <a id="27855" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27775" class="Bound">x</a><a id="27856" class="Symbol">))</a>
    <a id="27863" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27865" href="elementary-number-theory.equality-natural-numbers.html#3107" class="Function">is-decidable-is-zero-ℕ&#39;</a> <a id="27889" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27775" class="Bound">x</a><a id="27890" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="27892" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27691" class="Function">is-decidable-div-ℕ</a> <a id="27911" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27912" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="27919" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27919" class="Bound">d</a><a id="27920" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27922" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27922" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="27924" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="27928" href="foundation.decidable-types.html#5063" class="Function">is-decidable-iff</a>
    <a id="27949" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27951" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#5165" class="Function">div-is-zero-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="27974" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27919" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="27976" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27922" class="Bound">x</a><a id="27977" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="27983" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27985" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#4958" class="Function">is-zero-mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="28004" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27919" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="28006" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27922" class="Bound">x</a><a id="28007" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="28013" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28015" href="univalent-combinatorics.equality-standard-finite-types.html#3151" class="Function">is-decidable-is-zero-Fin</a> <a id="28040" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28041" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#2844" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕ</a> <a id="28052" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27919" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="28054" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27922" class="Bound">x</a><a id="28055" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="div-ℕ-decidable-Prop"></a><a id="28059" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28059" class="Function">div-ℕ-decidable-Prop</a> <a id="28080" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28082" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28083" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28083" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="28085" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28085" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="28087" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28089" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="28090" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28092" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28094" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1939" class="Function">is-nonzero-ℕ</a> <a id="28107" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28083" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="28109" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28111" href="foundation.decidable-propositions.html#2032" class="Function">decidable-Prop</a> <a id="28126" href="Agda.Primitive.html#764" class="Primitive">lzero</a>
<a id="28132" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="28136" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28137" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28059" class="Function">div-ℕ-decidable-Prop</a> <a id="28158" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28158" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="28160" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28160" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="28162" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28162" class="Bound">H</a><a id="28163" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28165" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="28167" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers.html#1608" class="Function">div-ℕ</a> <a id="28173" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28158" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="28175" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28160" class="Bound">x</a>
<a id="28177" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="28181" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28182" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="28186" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28187" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28059" class="Function">div-ℕ-decidable-Prop</a> <a id="28208" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28208" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="28210" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28210" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="28212" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28212" class="Bound">H</a><a id="28213" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="28216" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="28218" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers.html#2941" class="Function">is-prop-div-ℕ</a> <a id="28232" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28208" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="28234" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28210" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="28236" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28212" class="Bound">H</a>
<a id="28238" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="28242" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28243" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="28247" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28248" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28059" class="Function">div-ℕ-decidable-Prop</a> <a id="28269" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28269" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="28271" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28271" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="28273" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28273" class="Bound">H</a><a id="28274" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="28277" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="28279" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27691" class="Function">is-decidable-div-ℕ</a> <a id="28298" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28269" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="28300" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28271" class="Bound">x</a>

<a id="is-decidable-is-even-ℕ"></a><a id="28303" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28303" class="Function">is-decidable-is-even-ℕ</a> <a id="28326" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28328" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28329" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28329" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="28331" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28333" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="28334" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28336" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28338" href="foundation.decidable-types.html#1918" class="Function">is-decidable</a> <a id="28351" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28352" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers.html#2375" class="Function">is-even-ℕ</a> <a id="28362" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28329" class="Bound">x</a><a id="28363" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="28365" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28303" class="Function">is-decidable-is-even-ℕ</a> <a id="28388" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28388" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="28390" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="28392" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#27691" class="Function">is-decidable-div-ℕ</a> <a id="28411" class="Number">2</a> <a id="28413" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28388" class="Bound">x</a>

<a id="is-decidable-is-odd-ℕ"></a><a id="28416" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28416" class="Function">is-decidable-is-odd-ℕ</a> <a id="28438" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28440" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28441" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28441" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="28443" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28445" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="28446" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28448" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28450" href="foundation.decidable-types.html#1918" class="Function">is-decidable</a> <a id="28463" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28464" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers.html#2425" class="Function">is-odd-ℕ</a> <a id="28473" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28441" class="Bound">x</a><a id="28474" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>
<pre class="Agda"><a id="neg-neg-Fin"></a><a id="28559" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28559" class="Function">neg-neg-Fin</a> <a id="28571" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="28575" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28576" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28576" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="28578" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28580" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="28581" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28583" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28584" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28584" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="28586" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28588" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="28592" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28576" class="Bound">k</a><a id="28593" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28595" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28597" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7873" class="Function">neg-Fin</a> <a id="28605" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28606" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7873" class="Function">neg-Fin</a> <a id="28614" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28584" class="Bound">x</a><a id="28615" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28617" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="28619" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28584" class="Bound">x</a>
<a id="28621" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28559" class="Function">neg-neg-Fin</a> <a id="28633" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28634" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="28641" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28641" class="Bound">k</a><a id="28642" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28644" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28644" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="28646" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="28650" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28652" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="28656" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28657" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#10493" class="Function">right-unit-law-add-Fin</a> <a id="28680" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28681" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7873" class="Function">neg-Fin</a> <a id="28689" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28690" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7873" class="Function">neg-Fin</a> <a id="28698" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28644" class="Bound">x</a><a id="28699" class="Symbol">))))</a> <a id="28704" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
  <a id="28708" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28710" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28712" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="28715" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28716" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6113" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="28724" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28725" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7873" class="Function">neg-Fin</a> <a id="28733" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28734" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7873" class="Function">neg-Fin</a> <a id="28742" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28644" class="Bound">x</a><a id="28743" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="28747" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28748" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="28752" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28753" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#11177" class="Function">left-inverse-law-add-Fin</a> <a id="28778" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28644" class="Bound">x</a><a id="28779" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="28783" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
    <a id="28789" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28791" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28793" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="28797" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28798" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#9260" class="Function">associative-add-Fin</a> <a id="28818" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28819" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7873" class="Function">neg-Fin</a> <a id="28827" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28828" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7873" class="Function">neg-Fin</a> <a id="28836" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28644" class="Bound">x</a><a id="28837" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="28840" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28841" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7873" class="Function">neg-Fin</a> <a id="28849" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28644" class="Bound">x</a><a id="28850" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28852" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28644" class="Bound">x</a><a id="28853" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="28856" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
      <a id="28864" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28866" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28868" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="28871" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28872" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6226" class="Function">add-Fin&#39;</a> <a id="28881" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28644" class="Bound">x</a><a id="28882" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28884" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28885" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#11177" class="Function">left-inverse-law-add-Fin</a> <a id="28910" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28911" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7873" class="Function">neg-Fin</a> <a id="28919" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28644" class="Bound">x</a><a id="28920" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="28924" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
        <a id="28934" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28936" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#10998" class="Function">left-unit-law-add-Fin</a> <a id="28958" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28644" class="Bound">x</a><a id="28959" class="Symbol">))))</a>

<a id="is-equiv-neg-Fin"></a><a id="28965" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28965" class="Function">is-equiv-neg-Fin</a> <a id="28982" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="28986" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28987" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28987" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="28989" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28991" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="28992" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28994" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28996" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1556" class="Function">is-equiv</a> <a id="29005" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29006" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#7873" class="Function">neg-Fin</a> <a id="29014" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="29015" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#28987" class="Bound">k</a><a id="29016" class="Symbol">})</a>
